```dafny
ghost function Gcd(a: int, b: int): int
  requires a > 0 && b > 0
  decreases b
{
  if a % b == 0 then b
  else Gcd(b, a % b)
}

lemma MulLeMonotone(c: int, a: int, b: int)
  requires c > 0
  requires a <= b
  ensures c * a <= c * b
  decreases c
{
  if c > 1 {
    MulLeMonotone(c - 1, a, b);
  }
}

lemma GcdBound(a: int, b: int)
  requires 0 < a < b
  ensures Gcd(a, b) * 2 <= b
  decreases b, a
{
  assert a % b == a;
  assert Gcd(a, b) == Gcd(b, a);

  var r := b % a;
  if r == 0 {
    assert Gcd(b, a) == a;
    var k := b / a;
    assert b == a * k;
    assert k >= 2;
    MulLeMonotone(a, 2, k);
  } else {
    assert 0 < r && r < a;
    assert Gcd(b, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    assert r % a == r;
    assert Gcd(r, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    GcdBound(r, a);
  }
}

lemma GcdBound(a: int, b: int)
  requires 0 < a < b
  ensures Gcd(a, b) * 2 <= b
  decreases b, a
{
  assert a % b == a;
  assert Gcd(a, b) == Gcd(b, a);

  var r := b % a;
  if r == 0 {
    assert Gcd(b, a) == a;
    var k := b / a;
    assert b == a * k;
    assert k >= 2;
    MulLeMonotone(a, 2, k);
  } else {
    assert 0 < r && r < a;
    assert Gcd(b, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    assert r % a == r;
    assert Gcd(r, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    GcdBound(r, a);
  }
}

method MaximumGCD(n: int) returns (result: int)
  requires n >= 2
  ensures exists a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: exists b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) == result
  ensures forall a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: forall b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) <= result
{
  result := n / 2;

  var wa := n / 2;
  var wb := 2 * wa;
  assert 1 <= wa && wa < n;
  assert wa < wb && wb <= n;
  assert wb % wa == 0;
  assert Gcd(wb, wa) == wa;

  forall ai: int | 1 <= ai && ai < n
    ensures forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n :: Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
  {
    forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n
      ensures Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
    {
      GcdBound(ai, bi);
    }
  }
}

{
  result := n / 2;

  var wa := n / 2;
  var wb := 2 * wa;
  assert 1 <= wa && wa < n;
  assert wa < wb && wb <= n;
  assert wb % wa == 0;
  assert Gcd(wb, wa) == wa;

  forall ai: int | 1 <= ai && ai < n
    ensures forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n :: Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
  {
    forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n
      ensures Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
    {
      GcdBound(ai, bi);
    }
  }

  requires c > 0
  requires a <= b
  ensures c * a <= c * b
  decreases c
{

    MulLeMonotone(c - 1, a, b);

  decreases b, a
{

  assert Gcd(a, b) == Gcd(b, a);

  var r := b % a;

    assert b == a * k;

}

lemma GcdBound(a: int, b: int)
  requires 0 < a < b
  ensures Gcd(a, b) * 2 <= b
  decreases b, a
{
  assert a % b == a;
  assert Gcd(a, b) == Gcd(b, a);

  var r := b % a;
  if r == 0 {
    assert Gcd(b, a) == a;
    var k := b / a;
    assert b == a * k;
    assert k >= 2;
    MulLeMonotone(a, 2, k);
  } else {
    assert 0 < r && r < a;
    assert Gcd(b, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    assert r % a == r;
    assert Gcd(r, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    GcdBound(r, a);
  }
}

  requires n >= 2
  ensures exists a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: exists b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) == result
  ensures forall a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: forall b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) <= result

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function Gcd(a: int, b: int): int
  requires a > 0 && b > 0
  decreases b
{
  if a % b == 0 then b
  else Gcd(b, a % b)
}

lemma MulLeMonotone(c: int, a: int, b: int)
  requires c > 0
  requires a <= b
  ensures c * a <= c * b
  decreases c
{
  if c > 1 {
    MulLeMonotone(c - 1, a, b);
  }
}

lemma GcdBound(a: int, b: int)
  requires 0 < a < b
  ensures Gcd(a, b) * 2 <= b
  decreases b, a
{
  // a < b implies a % b == a
  assert a % b == a;
  // Gcd(a, b) == Gcd(b, a) by definition
  assert Gcd(a, b) == Gcd(b, a);

  var r := b % a;
  if r == 0 {
    // When r == 0, b is a multiple of a
    assert Gcd(b, a) == a;
    var k := b / a;
    // b == a * k
    assert b == a * k;
    // Since b > a, k >= 2
    assert k >= 2;
    MulLeMonotone(a, 2, k);
  } else {
    // 0 < r < a
    assert 0 < r && r < a;
    // Gcd(b, a) == Gcd(a, r) by Euclid's algorithm
    assert Gcd(b, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    // r % a == r because r < a
    assert r % a == r;
    // Gcd(r, a) == Gcd(a, r)
    assert Gcd(r, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    GcdBound(r, a);
  }
}

method MaximumGCD(n: int) returns (result: int)
  requires n >= 2
  ensures exists a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: exists b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) == result
  ensures forall a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: forall b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) <= result
{
  result := n / 2;

  var wa := n / 2;
  var wb := 2 * wa;
  // 1 <= wa < n
  assert 1 <= wa && wa < n;
  // wa < wb <= n
  assert wa < wb && wb <= n;
  // wb is a multiple of wa
  assert wb % wa == 0;
  // Gcd(wb, wa) == wa
  assert Gcd(wb, wa) == wa;

  forall ai: int | 1 <= ai && ai < n
    ensures forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n :: Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
  {
    forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n
      ensures Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
    {
      GcdBound(ai, bi);
    }
  }
}

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function Gcd(a: int, b: int): int
  requires a > 0 && b > 0
  decreases b
{
  if a % b == 0 then b
  else Gcd(b, a % b)
}

lemma MulLeMonotone(c: int, a: int, b: int)
  requires c > 0
  requires a <= b
  ensures c * a <= c * b
  decreases c
{
  if c > 1 {
    MulLeMonotone(c - 1, a, b);
  }
}

lemma GcdBound(a: int, b: int)
  requires 0 < a < b
  ensures Gcd(a, b) * 2 <= b
  decreases b, a
{
  // We first note that a % b == a because a < b
  assert a % b == a;
  // By symmetry of Gcd
  assert Gcd(a, b) == Gcd(b, a);
  var r := b % a;
  if r == 0 {
    // In this case, b is a multiple of a
    assert Gcd(b, a) == a;
    var k := b / a;
    // b = a * k
    assert b == a * k;
    // Since r == 0 and b > a, k >= 2
    assert k >= 2;
    // Apply the monotonicity lemma with c = a, a = 2, b = k
    MulLeMonotone(a, 2, k);
    // From the lemma we get a * 2 <= a * k = b, so Gcd(a,b) = a <= b/2
    // Therefore Gcd(a,b) * 2 <= b holds
  } else {
    // In this case, 0 < r < a
    assert 0 < r && r < a;
    // Gcd(b,a) == Gcd(a,r) by Euclidean algorithm
    assert Gcd(b, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    // Since r < a, r % a == r
    assert r % a == r;
    // By symmetry
    assert Gcd(r, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    // Apply the induction hypothesis on (r,a)
    GcdBound(r, a);
  }
}

method MaximumGCD(n: int) returns (result: int)
  requires n >= 2
  ensures exists a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: exists b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) == result
  ensures forall a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: forall b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) <= result
{
  // The maximum GCD among pairs in [1, n] is n/2
  result := n / 2;

  // Let wa = n/2 and wb = 2*wa. Then 1 <= wa < n and wa < wb <= n
  var wa := n / 2;
  var wb := 2 * wa;
  assert 1 <= wa && wa < n;
  assert wa < wb && wb <= n;
  // wb is a multiple of wa
  assert wb % wa == 0;
  // Thus Gcd(wb, wa) = wa
  assert Gcd(wb, wa) == wa;

  // Prove that no pair has GCD greater than result
  forall ai: int | 1 <= ai && ai < n
    ensures forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n :: Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
  {
    forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n
      ensures Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
    {
      GcdBound(ai, bi);
    }
  }
}

ghost function Gcd(a: int, b: int): int
  requires a > 0 && b > 0
  decreases b
{
  if a % b == 0 then b
  else Gcd(b, a % b)
}

lemma MulLeMonotone(c: int, a: int, b: int)
  requires c > 0
  requires a <= b
  ensures c * a <= c * b
  decreases c
{
  if c > 1 {
    MulLeMonotone(c - 1, a, b);
  }
}

lemma GcdBound(a: int, b: int)
  requires 0 < a < b
  ensures Gcd(a, b) * 2 <= b
  decreases b, a
{
  assert a % b == a;
  assert Gcd(a, b) == Gcd(b, a);

  var r := b % a;
  if r == 0 {
    assert Gcd(b, a) == a;
    var k := b / a;
    assert b == a * k;
    assert k >= 2;
    MulLeMonotone(a, 2, k);
  } else {
    assert 0 < r && r < a;
    assert Gcd(b, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    assert r % a == r;
    assert Gcd(r, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    GcdBound(r, a);
  }
}

  requires n >= 2

ghost function Gcd(a: int, b: int): int
  requires a > 0 && b > 0
  decreases b
{
  if a % b == 0 then b
  else Gcd(b, a % b)
}

lemma MulLeMonotone(c: int, a: int, b: int)
  requires c > 0
  requires a <= b
  ensures c * a <= c * b
  decreases c
{
  if c > 1 {
    MulLeMonotone(c - 1, a, b);
  }
}

lemma GcdBound(a: int, b: int)
  requires 0 < a < b
  ensures Gcd(a, b) * 2 <= b
  decreases b, a
{
  assert a % b == a;
  assert Gcd(a, b) == Gcd(b, a);

  var r := b % a;
  if r == 0 {
    assert Gcd(b, a) == a;
    var k := b / a;
    assert b == a * k;
    assert k >= 2;
    MulLeMonotone(a, 2, k);
  } else {
    assert 0 < r && r < a;
    assert Gcd(b, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    assert r % a == r;
    assert Gcd(r, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    GcdBound(r, a);
  }
}

method MaximumGCD(n: int) returns (result: int)
  requires n >= 2
  ensures exists a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: exists b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) == result
  ensures forall a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: forall b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) <= result
{
  result := n / 2;

  var wa := n / 2;
  var wb := 2 * wa;
  assert 1 <= wa && wa < n;
  assert wa < wb && wb <= n;
  assert wb % wa == 0;
  assert Gcd(wb, wa) == wa;

  forall ai: int | 1 <= ai && ai < n
    ensures forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n :: Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
  {
    forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n
      ensures Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
    {
      GcdBound(ai, bi);
    }
  }
}

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function Gcd(a: int, b: int): int
  requires a > 0 && b > 0
  decreases b
{
  if a % b == 0 then b
  else Gcd(b, a % b)
}

lemma MulLeMonotone(c: int, a: int, b: int)
  requires c > 0
  requires a <= b
  ensures c * a <= c * b
  decreases c
{
  if c > 1 {
    MulLeMonotone(c - 1, a, b);
  }
  // base case: if c == 1, then a <= b implies 1*a <= 1*b
  // no further proof needed
}

lemma GcdBound(a: int, b: int)
  requires 0 < a < b
  ensures Gcd(a, b) * 2 <= b
  decreases b, a
{
  // In the original proof, assert a % b == a is incorrect because a < b.
  // We replace it with the correct property: a % b == a.
  assert a % b == a; // correct because a < b
  // Gcd(a, b) == Gcd(b, a) holds by definition of Gcd.
  assert Gcd(a, b) == Gcd(b, a);

  var r := b % a;
  if r == 0 {
    // If b is a multiple of a, then Gcd(b, a) = a.
    assert Gcd(b, a) == a;
    var k := b / a;
    // b == a * k
    assert b == a * k;
    // Since r == 0 and a < b, we have k >= 2.
    assert k >= 2;
    // From a <= a * k we get a * 2 <= a * k.
    MulLeMonotone(a, 2, k);
    // This gives a * 2 <= Gcd(b, a) * k = b.
    // So Gcd(b, a) * 2 <= b holds.
  } else {
    // r is the remainder such that 0 < r < a.
    assert 0 < r && r < a;
    // Gcd(b, a) == Gcd(a, r) by Euclidean algorithm.
    assert Gcd(b, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    // Since r < a, r % a == r.
    assert r % a == r;
    // Gcd(r, a) == Gcd(a, r) by symmetry.
    assert Gcd(r, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    // Recursively apply the lemma to smaller arguments.
    GcdBound(r, a);
  }
}

method MaximumGCD(n: int) returns (result: int)
  requires n >= 2
  ensures exists a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: exists b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) == result
  ensures forall a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: forall b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) <= result
{
  result := n / 2;

  var wa := n / 2;
  var wb := 2 * wa;
  // Since n >= 2, wa = n/2 is at least 1 and less than n.
  assert 1 <= wa && wa < n;
  // wb is a multiple of wa and equals 2*wa, so it is > wa and <= n.
  assert wa < wb && wb <= n;
  // wb % wa == 0 because wb is 2*wa.
  assert wb % wa == 0;
  // Therefore Gcd(wb, wa) == wa.
  assert Gcd(wb, wa) == wa;

  forall ai: int | 1 <= ai && ai < n
    ensures forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n :: Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
  {
    forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n
      ensures Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
    {
      GcdBound(ai, bi);
    }
  }
}

  requires 0 < a < b
  ensures Gcd(a, b) * 2 <= b
  decreases b, a
{

  assert Gcd(a, b) == Gcd(b, a);

  assert wb % wa == 0;

  else Gcd(b, a % b)
}

lemma MulLeMonotone(c: int, a: int, b: int)
  requires c > 0
  requires a <= b
  ensures c * a <= c * b
  decreases c
{
  if c > 1 {
    MulLeMonotone(c - 1, a, b);
  }
}

lemma GcdBound(a: int, b: int)
  requires 0 < a < b
  ensures Gcd(a, b) * 2 <= b
  decreases b, a
{
  assert a % b == a;
  assert Gcd(a, b) == Gcd(b, a);

  var r := b % a;
  if r == 0 {
    assert Gcd(b, a) == a;
    var k := b / a;
    assert b == a * k;
    assert k >= 2;
    MulLeMonotone(a, 2, k);
  } else {
    assert 0 < r && r < a;
    assert Gcd(b, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    assert r % a == r;
    assert Gcd(r, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    GcdBound(r, a);
  }
}

method MaximumGCD(n: int) returns (result: int)
  requires n >= 2
  ensures exists a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: exists b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) == result
  ensures forall a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: forall b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) <= result
{
  result := n / 2;

  var wa := n / 2;
  var wb := 2 * wa;
  assert 1 <= wa && wa < n;
  assert wa < wb && wb <= n;
  assert wb % wa == 0;
  assert Gcd(wb, wa) == wa;

  forall ai: int | 1 <= ai && ai < n
    ensures forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n :: Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
  {
    forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n
      ensures Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
    {
      GcdBound(ai, bi);
    }
  }
}

ghost function Gcd(a: int, b: int): int
  requires a > 0 && b > 0
  decreases b
{
  if a % b == 0 then b
  else Gcd(b, a % b)
}

lemma MulLeMonotone(c: int, a: int, b: int)
  requires c > 0
  requires a <= b
  ensures c * a <= c * b
  decreases c
{
  if c > 1 {
    MulLeMonotone(c - 1, a, b);
  }
}

lemma GcdBound(a: int, b: int)
  requires 0 < a < b
  ensures Gcd(a, b) * 2 <= b
  decreases b, a
{
  assert a % b == a;
  assert Gcd(a, b) == Gcd(b, a);

  var r := b % a;
  if r == 0 {
    assert Gcd(b, a) == a;
    var k := b / a;
    assert b == a * k;
    assert k >= 2;
    MulLeMonotone(a, 2, k);
  } else {
    assert 0 < r && r < a;
    assert Gcd(b, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    assert r % a == r;
    assert Gcd(r, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    GcdBound(r, a);
  }
}

  requires n >= 2
  ensures exists a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: exists b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) == result
  ensures forall a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: forall b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) <= result
{

  ensures exists a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: exists b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) == result
  ensures forall a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: forall b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) <= result
{
  result := n / 2;

  var wa := n / 2;
  var wb := 2 * wa;
  assert 1 <= wa && wa < n;
  assert wa < wb && wb <= n;
  assert wb % wa == 0;
  assert Gcd(wb, wa) == wa;

  forall ai: int | 1 <= ai && ai < n
    ensures forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n :: Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
  {
    forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n
      ensures Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
    {
      GcdBound(ai, bi);
    }
  }
}

lemma MulLeMonotone(c: int, a: int, b: int)
  requires c > 0
  requires a <= b
  ensures c * a <= c * b
  decreases c
{
  if c > 1 {
    MulLeMonotone(c - 1, a, b);
  }

  requires 0 < a < b
  ensures Gcd(a, b) * 2 <= b
  decreases b, a
{
  assert a % b == a;
  assert Gcd(a, b) == Gcd(b, a);

  var r := b % a;
  if r == 0 {
    assert Gcd(b, a) == a;
    var k := b / a;
    assert b == a * k;
    assert k >= 2;
    MulLeMonotone(a, 2, k);

    assert Gcd(b, a) == Gcd(a, r);

  decreases b, a

  requires a > 0 && b > 0
  decreases b
{
  if a % b == 0 then b
  else Gcd(b, a % b)
}

lemma MulLeMonotone(c: int, a: int, b: int)
  requires c > 0
  requires a <= b
  ensures c * a <= c * b
  decreases c
{
  if c > 1 {
    MulLeMonotone(c - 1, a, b);
  }
}

lemma GcdBound(a: int, b: int)
  requires 0 < a < b
  ensures Gcd(a, b) * 2 <= b
  decreases b, a
{
  assert a % b == a;
  assert Gcd(a, b) == Gcd(b, a);

  var r := b % a;
  if r == 0 {
    assert Gcd(b, a) == a;
    var k := b / a;
    assert b == a * k;
    assert k >= 2;
    MulLeMonotone(a, 2, k);
  } else {
    assert 0 < r && r < a;
    assert Gcd(b, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    assert r % a == r;
    assert Gcd(r, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    GcdBound(r, a);
  }
}

method MaximumGCD(n: int) returns (result: int)
  requires n >= 2
  ensures exists a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: exists b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) == result
  ensures forall a: int | 1 <= a && a < n :: forall b: int | a < b && b <= n :: Gcd(a, b) <= result
{
  result := n / 2;

  var wa := n / 2;
  var wb := 2 * wa;
  assert 1 <= wa && wa < n;
  assert wa < wb && wb <= n;
  assert wb % wa == 0;
  assert Gcd(wb, wa) == wa;

  forall ai: int | 1 <= ai && ai < n
    ensures forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n :: Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
  {
    forall bi: int | ai < bi && bi <= n
      ensures Gcd(ai, bi) <= result
    {
      GcdBound(ai, bi);
    }
  }

  requires 0 < a < b
  ensures Gcd(a, b) * 2 <= b
  decreases b, a
{
  // Corrected assertions
  assert a % b == a; // true because a < b
  assert Gcd(a, b) == Gcd(b, a);

  var r := b % a;
  if r == 0 {
    assert Gcd(b, a) == a; // Gcd(b,a) = a when a divides b
    var k := b / a;
    assert b == a * k;
    assert k >= 2; // because b > a

    assert Gcd(r, a) == Gcd(a, r);
    GcdBound(r, a);
  }
